\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00003}00003 \textcolor{comment}{/*-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00004}00004 \textcolor{comment}{   Interface to distributed SuperLU, created by JWB by adapting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00005}00005 \textcolor{comment}{   code in the superlu distribution, i.e. files /SRC/pdgssvx.c}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00006}00006 \textcolor{comment}{   (function pdgssvx solves a system of linear equations) and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00007}00007 \textcolor{comment}{   /EXAMPLE/pddrive.c demo (a driver program to illustrate how to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00008}00008 \textcolor{comment}{   use pdgssvx).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00009}00009 \textcolor{comment}{   Essentially the code below performs the same functions as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00010}00010 \textcolor{comment}{   pdgssvx in a modified order which allows resolves. Much of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00011}00011 \textcolor{comment}{   code taken from pdgssvx remains essentially unchanged other}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00012}00012 \textcolor{comment}{   than changing the layout to match the oomph-\/lib standard. Comments}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00013}00013 \textcolor{comment}{   from the original code have been left unchanged whenever possible}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00014}00014 \textcolor{comment}{   to help match this code with that found in pdgssvx.c}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00015}00015 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00016}00016 \textcolor{comment}{   To update this driver code for use with later versions of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00017}00017 \textcolor{comment}{   Distributed SuperLU I suggest first looking at changes (if any) to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00018}00018 \textcolor{comment}{   the two distributed SuperLU files, and then making the corresponding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00019}00019 \textcolor{comment}{   changes to the code below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00020}00020 \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00128}00128 \textcolor{comment}{/*-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00129}00129 \textcolor{comment}{   Bridge to distributed SuperLU with distributed memory (version 2.0).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00130}00130 \textcolor{comment}{   Requires input of system matrix in compressed row form.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00131}00131 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00132}00132 \textcolor{comment}{   Parameters:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00133}00133 \textcolor{comment}{   op\_flag    = int specifies the operation:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00134}00134 \textcolor{comment}{                  1, performs LU decomposition for the first time}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00135}00135 \textcolor{comment}{                  2, performs triangular solve}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00136}00136 \textcolor{comment}{                  3, free all the storage in the end}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00137}00137 \textcolor{comment}{   -\/ n = size of system (square matrix)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00138}00138 \textcolor{comment}{   -\/ nnz = \# of nonzero entries}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00139}00139 \textcolor{comment}{   -\/ values = 1D C array of nonzero entries}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00140}00140 \textcolor{comment}{   -\/ row\_index =  1D C array of row indices}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00141}00141 \textcolor{comment}{   -\/ column\_start =  1D C array of column start indices}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00142}00142 \textcolor{comment}{   -\/ b = 1D C array representing the rhs vector, is overwritten}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00143}00143 \textcolor{comment}{         by solution.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00144}00144 \textcolor{comment}{   -\/ nprow = \# of rows in process grid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00145}00145 \textcolor{comment}{   -\/ npcol = \# of columns in process grid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00146}00146 \textcolor{comment}{   -\/ doc = 0/1 for doc/no doc}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l00147}00147 \textcolor{comment}{   -\/ data  = pointer to structure to contain LU solver data.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l01209}01209 \textcolor{comment}{                  1, performs LU decomposition for the first time}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l01210}01210 \textcolor{comment}{                  2, performs triangular solve}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l01211}01211 \textcolor{comment}{                  3, free all the storage in the end}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l01212}01212 \textcolor{comment}{   -\/ n = size of system (square matrix)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l01213}01213 \textcolor{comment}{   -\/ nnz = \# of nonzero entries}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l01215}01215 \textcolor{comment}{   -\/ row\_index =  1D C array of row indices}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l01216}01216 \textcolor{comment}{   -\/ column\_start =  1D C array of column start indices}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l01217}01217 \textcolor{comment}{   -\/ b = 1D C array representing the rhs vector, is overwritten}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l01218}01218 \textcolor{comment}{         by solution.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l01219}01219 \textcolor{comment}{   -\/ nprow = \# of rows in process grid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l01220}01220 \textcolor{comment}{   -\/ npcol = \# of columns in process grid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l01221}01221 \textcolor{comment}{   -\/ doc = 0/1 for doc/no doc}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l01222}01222 \textcolor{comment}{   -\/ data  = pointer to structure to contain LU solver data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l01223}01223 \textcolor{comment}{             If *opt\_flag == 1, it is an output. Otherwise, it it an input.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l01224}01224 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l01225}01225 \textcolor{comment}{   Return value of *info:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l01226}01226 \textcolor{comment}{           = 0: successful exit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l01227}01227 \textcolor{comment}{           > 0: if *info = i, and i is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l01228}01228 \textcolor{comment}{               <= A-\/>ncol: U(i,i) is exactly zero. The factorization has}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l01229}01229 \textcolor{comment}{                  been completed, but the factor U is exactly singular,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l01230}01230 \textcolor{comment}{                  so the solution could not be computed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l01231}01231 \textcolor{comment}{               > A-\/>ncol: number of bytes allocated when memory allocation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l01232}01232 \textcolor{comment}{                  failure occurred, plus A-\/>ncol.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{superlu__dist_8c_source_l01233}01233 \textcolor{comment}{           < 0: some other error}}
